    28	import org.web3j.protocol.core.Response;
    29	
    30	/**
    31	 * Log object returned by:
    32	 *
    33	 * <ul>
    34	 *   <li>eth_getFilterChanges
    35	 *   <li>eth_getFilterLogs
    36	 *   <li>eth_getLogs
    37	 * </ul>
    38	 *
    39	 * <p>See <a href="https://github.com/ethereum/wiki/wiki/JSON-RPC#eth_getfilterchanges">docs</a> for
    40	 * further details.
    41	 */
    42	public class EthLog extends Response<List<EthLog.LogResult>> {
    43	
    44	    @Override
    45	    @JsonDeserialize(using = LogResultDeserialiser.class)
    46	    public void setResult(List<LogResult> result) {
    47	        super.setResult(result);
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    public List<LogResult> getLogs() {
    51	        return getResult();
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    public interface LogResult<T> {
    55	        T get();
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    public static class LogObject extends Log implements LogResult<Log> {
    59	
    60	        public LogObject() {}
    61	
    62	        public LogObject(
    63	                boolean removed,
    64	                String logIndex,
    65	                String transactionIndex,
    66	                String transactionHash,
    67	                String blockHash,
    68	                String blockNumber,
    69	                String address,
    70	                String data,
    71	                String type,
    72	                List<String> topics) {
    73	            super(
    74	                    removed,
    75	                    logIndex,
    76	                    transactionIndex,
    77	                    transactionHash,
    78	                    blockHash,
    79	                    blockNumber,
    80	                    address,
    81	                    data,
    82	                    type,
    83	                    topics);
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        @Override
    87	        public Log get() {
    88	            return this;
    89	        }
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    public static class Hash implements LogResult<String> {
    93	        private String value;
    94	
    95	        public Hash() {}
    96	
    97	        public Hash(String value) {
    98	            this.value = value;
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        @Override
   102	        public String get() {
   103	            return value;
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        public void setValue(String value) {
   107	            this.value = value;
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        @Override
   111	        public boolean equals(Object o) {
   112	            if (this == o) {
   113	                return true;
   114	            }
   115	            if (!(o instanceof Hash)) {
   116	                return false;
   117	            }
   118	
   119	            Hash hash = (Hash) o;
   120	
   121	            return value != null ? value.equals(hash.value) : hash.value == null;
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        @Override
   125	        public int hashCode() {
   126	            return value != null ? value.hashCode() : 0;
   127	        }
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    public static class LogResultDeserialiser extends JsonDeserializer<List<LogResult>> {
   131	
   132	        private ObjectReader objectReader = ObjectMapperFactory.getObjectReader();
   133	
   134	        @Override
   135	        public List<LogResult> deserialize(
   136	                JsonParser jsonParser, DeserializationContext deserializationContext)
   137	                throws IOException {
   138	
   139	            List<LogResult> logResults = new ArrayList<>();
   140	            JsonToken nextToken = jsonParser.nextToken();
   141	
   142	            if (nextToken == JsonToken.START_OBJECT) {
   143	                Iterator<LogObject> logObjectIterator =
   144	                        objectReader.readValues(jsonParser, LogObject.class);
   145	                while (logObjectIterator.hasNext()) {
   146	                    logResults.add(logObjectIterator.next());
   147	                }
   148	            } else if (nextToken == JsonToken.VALUE_STRING) {
   149	                jsonParser.getValueAsString();
   150	
   151	                Iterator<Hash> transactionHashIterator =
   152	                        objectReader.readValues(jsonParser, Hash.class);
   153	                while (transactionHashIterator.hasNext()) {
   154	                    logResults.add(transactionHashIterator.next());
   155	                }
   156	            }
   157	            return logResults;
   158	        }
   159	    }
   160	}

    13	package org.web3j.protocol.core.filters;
    14	
    15	import java.io.IOException;
    16	import java.math.BigInteger;
    17	import java.util.Collections;
    18	import java.util.List;
    19	import java.util.Optional;
    20	import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
    21	import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledFuture;
    22	import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
    23	import java.util.regex.Pattern;
    24	
    25	import org.slf4j.Logger;
    26	import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
    27	
    28	import org.web3j.protocol.Web3j;
    29	import org.web3j.protocol.core.Request;
    30	import org.web3j.protocol.core.Response;
    31	import org.web3j.protocol.core.Response.Error;
    32	import org.web3j.protocol.core.RpcErrors;
    33	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthFilter;
    34	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog;
    35	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthUninstallFilter;
    36	
    37	/** Class for creating managed filter requests with callbacks. */
    38	public abstract class Filter<T> {
    39	
    40	    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(Filter.class);
    41	
    42	    protected final Web3j web3j;
    43	    protected Callback<T> callback;
    44	
    45	    private volatile BigInteger filterId;
    46	
    47	    protected ScheduledFuture<?> schedule;
    48	
    49	    private ScheduledExecutorService scheduledExecutorService;
    50	
    51	    private long blockTime;
    52	
    53	    private static final String FILTER_NOT_FOUND_PATTERN = "(?i)\\bfilter\\s+not\\s+found\\b";
    54	
    55	    public Filter(Web3j web3j, Callback<T> callback) {
    56	        this.web3j = web3j;
    57	        this.callback = callback;
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    public void run(ScheduledExecutorService scheduledExecutorService, long blockTime) {
    61	        try {
    62	            EthFilter ethFilter = sendRequest();
    63	            if (ethFilter.hasError()) {
    64	                throwException(ethFilter.getError());
    65	            }
    66	
    67	            filterId = ethFilter.getFilterId();
    68	            this.scheduledExecutorService = scheduledExecutorService;
    69	            this.blockTime = blockTime;
    70	            // this runs in the caller thread as if any exceptions are encountered, we shouldn't
    71	            // proceed with creating the scheduled task below
    72	            getInitialFilterLogs();
    73	
    74	            /*
    75	            We want the filter to be resilient against client issues. On numerous occasions
    76	            users have reported socket timeout exceptions when connected over HTTP to Geth and
    77	            Parity clients. For examples, refer to
    78	            https://github.com/web3j/web3j/issues/144 and
    79	            https://github.com/ethereum/go-ethereum/issues/15243.
    80	
    81	            Hence we consume errors and log them as errors, allowing our polling for changes to
    82	            resume. The downside of this approach is that users will not be notified of
    83	            downstream connection issues. But given the intermittent nature of the connection
    84	            issues, this seems like a reasonable compromise.
    85	
    86	            The alternative approach would be to have another thread that blocks waiting on
    87	            schedule.get(), catching any Exceptions thrown, and passing them back up to the
    88	            caller. However, the user would then be required to recreate subscriptions manually
    89	            which isn't ideal given the aforementioned issues.
    90	            */
    91	            schedule =
    92	                    scheduledExecutorService.scheduleAtFixedRate(
    93	                            () -> {
    94	                                try {
    95	                                    this.pollFilter(ethFilter);
    96	                                } catch (Throwable e) {
    97	                                    // All exceptions must be caught, otherwise our job terminates
    98	                                    // without
    99	                                    // any notification
   100	                                    log.warn("Error sending request", e);
   101	                                }
   102	                            },
   103	                            0,
   104	                            blockTime,
   105	                            TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
   106	        } catch (IOException e) {
   107	            throwException(e);
   108	        }
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    private void getInitialFilterLogs() {
   112	        try {
   113	            Optional<Request<?, EthLog>> maybeRequest = this.getFilterLogs(this.filterId);
   114	            EthLog ethLog = null;
   115	            if (maybeRequest.isPresent()) {
   116	                ethLog = maybeRequest.get().send();
   117	            } else {
   118	                ethLog = new EthLog();
   119	                ethLog.setResult(Collections.emptyList());
   120	            }
   121	
   122	            if (ethLog.hasError()) {
   123	                throwException(ethLog.getError());
   124	            }
   125	
   126	            process(ethLog.getLogs());
   127	
   128	        } catch (IOException e) {
   129	            throwException(e);
   130	        }
   131	    }
   132	
   133	    private void pollFilter(EthFilter ethFilter) {
   134	        EthLog ethLog = null;
   135	        try {
   136	            ethLog = web3j.ethGetFilterChanges(filterId).send();
   137	        } catch (IOException e) {
   138	            throwException(e);
   139	        }
   140	        if (ethLog.hasError()) {
   141	            Error error = ethLog.getError();
   142	            String message = error.getMessage();
   143	            switch (error.getCode()) {
   144	                case RpcErrors.FILTER_NOT_FOUND:
   145	                    reinstallFilter();
   146	                    break;
   147	                default:
   148	                    if (Pattern.compile(FILTER_NOT_FOUND_PATTERN).matcher(message).find())
   149	                        reinstallFilter();
   150	                    else throwException(error);
   151	                    break;
   152	            }
   153	        } else {
   154	            process(ethLog.getLogs());
   155	        }
   156	    }
   157	
   158	    protected abstract EthFilter sendRequest() throws IOException;
   159	
   160	    protected abstract void process(List<EthLog.LogResult> logResults);
   161	
   162	    private void reinstallFilter() {
   163	        log.warn(
   164	                "Previously installed filter has not been found, trying to re-install. Filter id: {}",
   165	                filterId);
   166	        schedule.cancel(false);
   167	        this.run(scheduledExecutorService, blockTime);
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    public void cancel() {
   171	        schedule.cancel(false);
   172	
   173	        try {
   174	            EthUninstallFilter ethUninstallFilter = uninstallFilter(filterId);
   175	            if (ethUninstallFilter.hasError()) {
   176	                throwException(ethUninstallFilter.getError());
   177	            }
   178	
   179	            if (!ethUninstallFilter.isUninstalled()) {
   180	                throw new FilterException("Filter with id '" + filterId + "' failed to uninstall");
   181	            }
   182	        } catch (IOException e) {
   183	            throwException(e);
   184	        }
   185	    }
   186	
   187	    protected EthUninstallFilter uninstallFilter(BigInteger filterId) throws IOException {
   188	        return web3j.ethUninstallFilter(filterId).send();
   189	    }
   190	
   191	    /**
   192	     * Retrieves historic filters for the filter with the given id. Getting historic logs is not
   193	     * supported by all filters. If not the method should return an empty EthLog object
   194	     *
   195	     * @param filterId Id of the filter for which the historic log should be retrieved
   196	     * @return Historic logs, or an empty optional if the filter cannot retrieve historic logs
   197	     */
   198	    protected abstract Optional<Request<?, EthLog>> getFilterLogs(BigInteger filterId);
   199	
   200	    void throwException(Response.Error error) {
   201	        throw new FilterException(
   202	                "Invalid request: " + (error == null ? "Unknown Error" : error.getMessage()));
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    void throwException(Throwable cause) {
   206	        throw new FilterException("Error sending request", cause);
   207	    }
   208	}

    13	package org.web3j.protocol.core.filters;
    14	
    15	import java.io.IOException;
    16	import java.math.BigInteger;
    17	import java.util.ArrayList;
    18	import java.util.List;
    19	import java.util.Optional;
    20	
    21	import org.web3j.protocol.Web3j;
    22	import org.web3j.protocol.core.Request;
    23	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthFilter;
    24	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog;
    25	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog.LogResult;
    26	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.Log;
    27	
    28	/** Logs filter handler. */
    29	public class LogsFilter extends Filter<List<Log>> {
    30	
    31	    private final org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.request.EthFilter ethFilter;
    32	
    33	    public LogsFilter(
    34	            Web3j web3j,
    35	            Callback<List<Log>> callback,
    36	            org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.request.EthFilter ethFilter) {
    37	        super(web3j, callback);
    38	        this.ethFilter = ethFilter;
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    @Override
    42	    protected EthFilter sendRequest() throws IOException {
    43	        return web3j.ethNewFilter(ethFilter).send();
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    @Override
    47	    protected void process(List<LogResult> logResults) {
    48	        List<Log> logs = new ArrayList<>(logResults.size());
    49	
    50	        for (EthLog.LogResult logResult : logResults) {
    51	            if (!(logResult instanceof EthLog.LogObject)) {
    52	                throw new FilterException(
    53	                        "Unexpected result type: " + logResult.get() + " required LogObject");
    54	            }
    55	
    56	            logs.add(((EthLog.LogObject) logResult).get());
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        callback.onEvent(logs);
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    @Override
    63	    protected Optional<Request<?, EthLog>> getFilterLogs(BigInteger filterId) {
    64	        return Optional.of(web3j.ethGetFilterLogs(filterId));
    65	    }
    66	}

    13	package org.web3j.protocol.core.filters;
    14	
    15	import java.io.IOException;
    16	import java.math.BigInteger;
    17	import java.util.List;
    18	import java.util.Optional;
    19	
    20	import org.web3j.protocol.Web3j;
    21	import org.web3j.protocol.core.Request;
    22	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthFilter;
    23	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog;
    24	
    25	/** Handler for working with block filter requests. */
    26	public class BlockFilter extends Filter<String> {
    27	
    28	    public BlockFilter(Web3j web3j, Callback<String> callback) {
    29	        super(web3j, callback);
    30	    }
    31	
    32	    @Override
    33	    protected EthFilter sendRequest() throws IOException {
    34	        return web3j.ethNewBlockFilter().send();
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    @Override
    38	    protected void process(List<EthLog.LogResult> logResults) {
    39	        for (EthLog.LogResult logResult : logResults) {
    40	            if (logResult instanceof EthLog.Hash) {
    41	                String blockHash = ((EthLog.Hash) logResult).get();
    42	                callback.onEvent(blockHash);
    43	            } else {
    44	                throw new FilterException(
    45	                        "Unexpected result type: " + logResult.get() + ", required Hash");
    46	            }
    47	        }
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    /**
    51	     * Since the block filter does not support historic filters, the filterId is ignored and an
    52	     * empty optional is returned.
    53	     *
    54	     * @param filterId Id of the filter for which the historic log should be retrieved
    55	     * @return Optional.empty()
    56	     */
    57	    @Override
    58	    protected Optional<Request<?, EthLog>> getFilterLogs(BigInteger filterId) {
    59	        return Optional.empty();
    60	    }
    61	}

    32	            Web3j web3j,

    25	
    26	/** Handler hashes for working with transaction filter requests. */
    27	public class PendingTransactionsFilter extends Filter<List<String>> {
    28	
    29	    public PendingTransactionsFilter(Web3j web3j, Callback<List<String>> callback) {
    30	        super(web3j, callback);
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    @Override
    34	    protected EthFilter sendRequest() throws IOException {
    35	        return web3j.ethNewPendingTransactionFilter().send();
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    @Override
    39	    protected void process(List<EthLog.LogResult> logResults) {
    40	        List<String> logs = new ArrayList<>(logResults.size());
    41	
    42	        for (EthLog.LogResult logResult : logResults) {
    43	            if (!(logResult instanceof EthLog.Hash)) {
    44	                throw new FilterException(
    45	                        "Unexpected result type: " + logResult.get() + ", required Hash");
    46	            }
    47	
    48	            logs.add(((EthLog.Hash) logResult).get());
    49	        }
    50	
    51	        callback.onEvent(logs);
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    /**
    55	     * Since the pending transaction filter does not support historic filters, the filterId is
    56	     * ignored and an empty optional is returned
    57	     *
    58	     * @param filterId Id of the filter for which the historic log should be retrieved
    59	     * @return Optional.empty()
    60	     */
    61	    @Override
    62	    protected Optional<Request<?, EthLog>> getFilterLogs(BigInteger filterId) {
    63	        return Optional.empty();
    64	    }
    65	}

    43

    47	        super.setResult(result);
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    public List<LogResult> getLogs() {
    51	        return getResult();
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    public interface LogResult<T> {
    55	        T get();
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    public static class LogObject extends Log implements LogResult<Log> {
    59	
    60	        public LogObject() {}
    61	
    62	        public LogObject(
    63	                boolean removed,
    64	                String logIndex,
    65	                String transactionIndex,
    66	                String transactionHash,

    69	                String address,
    70	                String data,

    72	                List<String> topics) {
    73	            super(
    74	                    removed,
    75	                    logIndex,
    76	                    transactionIndex,
    77	                    transactionHash,
    78	                    blockHash,
    79	                    blockNumber,
    80	                    address,
    81	                    data,
    82	                    type,
    83	                    topics);
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        @Override
    87	        public Log get() {
    88	            return this;
    89	        }
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    public static class Hash implements LogResult<String> {
    93	        private String value;
    94	
    95	        public Hash() {}
    96	
    97	        public Hash(String value) {
    98	            this.value = value;
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        @Override
   102	        public String get() {
   103	            return value;
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        public void setValue(String value) {
   107	            this.value = value;
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        @Override
   111	        public boolean equals(Object o) {
   112	            if (this == o) {
   113	                return true;
   114	            }
   115	            if (!(o instanceof Hash)) {
   116	                return false;
   117	            }
   118	
   119	            Hash hash = (Hash) o;
   120	
   121	            return value != null ? value.equals(hash.value) : hash.value == null;
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        @Override
   125	        public int hashCode() {
   126	            return value != null ? value.hashCode() : 0;
   127	        }
   128	    }
   129

   131

   133	
   134	        @Override
   135	        public List<LogResult> deserialize(
   136	                JsonParser jsonParser, DeserializationContext deserializationContext)
   137	                throws IOException {

    30	/**
    31	 * Log object returned by:
    32	 *
    33	 * <ul>
    34	 *   <li>eth_getFilterChanges

    36	 *   <li>eth_getLogs

    39	 * <p>See <a href="https://github.com/ethereum/wiki/wiki/JSON-RPC#eth_getfilterchanges">docs</a> for

    41	 */
    42	public class EthLog extends Response<List<EthLog.LogResult<?>>> {
    43	
    44	    @Override
    45	    @JsonDeserialize(using = LogResultDeserialiser.class)
    46	    public void setResult(List<LogResult<?>> result) {
    47	        super.setResult(result);
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    public List<LogResult<?>> getLogs() {
    51	        return getResult();
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    public interface LogResult<T> {
    55	        T get();
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    public static class LogObject extends Log implements LogResult<Log> {
    59	
    60	        public LogObject() {}
    61	
    62	        public LogObject(
    63	                boolean removed,
    64	                String logIndex,
    65	                String transactionIndex,
    66	                String transactionHash,
    67	                String blockHash,
    68	                String blockNumber,
    69	                String address,
    70	                String data,
    71	                String type,
    72	                List<String> topics) {
    73	            super(
    74	                    removed,
    75	                    logIndex,
    76	                    transactionIndex,
    77	                    transactionHash,
    78	                    blockHash,
    79	                    blockNumber,
    80	                    address,
    81	                    data,
    82	                    type,
    83	                    topics);
    84	        }
    85	
    86	        @Override
    87	        public Log get() {
    88	            return this;
    89	        }
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    public static class Hash implements LogResult<String> {
    93	        private String value;
    94	
    95	        public Hash() {}
    96	
    97	        public Hash(String value) {
    98	            this.value = value;
    99	        }
   100	
   101	        @Override
   102	        public String get() {
   103	            return value;
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        public void setValue(String value) {
   107	            this.value = value;
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        @Override
   111	        public boolean equals(Object o) {
   112	            if (this == o) {
   113	                return true;
   114	            }
   115	            if (!(o instanceof Hash)) {
   116	                return false;
   117	            }
   118	
   119	            Hash hash = (Hash) o;
   120	
   121	            return value != null ? value.equals(hash.value) : hash.value == null;
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        @Override
   125	        public int hashCode() {
   126	            return value != null ? value.hashCode() : 0;
   127	        }
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    public static class LogResultDeserialiser extends JsonDeserializer<List<LogResult<?>>> {
   131	
   132	        private ObjectReader objectReader = ObjectMapperFactory.getObjectReader();
   133	
   134	        @Override
   135	        public List<LogResult<?>> deserialize(
   136	                JsonParser jsonParser, DeserializationContext deserializationContext)
   137	                throws IOException {
   138	
   139	            List<LogResult<?>> logResults = new ArrayList<>();
   140	            JsonToken nextToken = jsonParser.nextToken();
   141	
   142	            if (nextToken == JsonToken.START_OBJECT) {
   143	                Iterator<LogObject> logObjectIterator =
   144	                        objectReader.readValues(jsonParser, LogObject.class);
   145	                while (logObjectIterator.hasNext()) {
   146	                    logResults.add(logObjectIterator.next());
   147	                }
   148	            } else if (nextToken == JsonToken.VALUE_STRING) {
   149	                jsonParser.getValueAsString();
   150	
   151	                Iterator<Hash> transactionHashIterator =
   152	                        objectReader.readValues(jsonParser, Hash.class);
   153	                while (transactionHashIterator.hasNext()) {
   154	                    logResults.add(transactionHashIterator.next());
   155	                }
   156	            }
   157	            return logResults;
   158	        }
   159	    }

    13	package org.web3j.protocol.core.filters;
    14	
    15	import java.io.IOException;
    16	import java.math.BigInteger;
    17	import java.util.ArrayList;
    18	import java.util.List;
    19	import java.util.Optional;
    20	
    21	import org.web3j.protocol.Web3j;
    22	import org.web3j.protocol.core.Request;
    23	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthFilter;
    24	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog;
    25	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog.LogResult;
    26	
    27	/** Handler hashes for working with block filter requests */
    28	public class BlocksFilter extends Filter<List<String>> {
    29	
    30	    public BlocksFilter(Web3j web3j, Callback<List<String>> callback) {
    31	        super(web3j, callback);
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    @Override
    35	    protected EthFilter sendRequest() throws IOException {
    36	        return web3j.ethNewBlockFilter().send();
    37	    }
    38	
    39	    @Override
    40	    protected void process(List<LogResult> logResults) {
    41	        List<String> blockHashes = new ArrayList<>(logResults.size());
    42	
    43	        for (EthLog.LogResult logResult : logResults) {
    44	            if (!(logResult instanceof EthLog.Hash)) {
    45	                throw new FilterException(
    46	                        "Unexpected result type: " + logResult.get() + ", required Hash");
    47	            }
    48	
    49	            blockHashes.add(((EthLog.Hash) logResult).get());
    50	        }
    51	
    52	        callback.onEvent(blockHashes);
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    /**
    56	     * Since the block filter does not support historic filters, the filterId is ignored and an
    57	     * empty optional is returned.
    58	     *
    59	     * @param filterId Id of the filter for which the historic log should be retrieved
    60	     * @return Optional.empty()
    61	     */
    62	    @Override
    63	    protected Optional<Request<?, EthLog>> getFilterLogs(BigInteger filterId) {
    64	        return Optional.empty();
    65	    }
    66	}

    13	package org.web3j.protocol.core.filters;
    14	
    15	import java.io.IOException;
    16	import java.math.BigInteger;
    17	import java.util.ArrayList;
    18	import java.util.List;
    19	import java.util.Optional;
    20	
    21	import org.web3j.protocol.Web3j;
    22	import org.web3j.protocol.core.Request;
    23	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthFilter;
    24	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog;
    25	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog.LogResult;
    26	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.Log;
    27	
    28	/** Logs filter handler. */
    29	public class LogsFilter extends Filter<List<Log>> {
    30	
    31	    private final org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.request.EthFilter ethFilter;
    32	
    33	    public LogsFilter(
    34	            Web3j web3j,
    35	            Callback<List<Log>> callback,
    36	            org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.request.EthFilter ethFilter) {
    37	        super(web3j, callback);
    38	        this.ethFilter = ethFilter;
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    @Override
    42	    protected EthFilter sendRequest() throws IOException {
    43	        return web3j.ethNewFilter(ethFilter).send();
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    @Override
    47	    protected void process(List<LogResult> logResults) {
    48	        List<Log> logs = new ArrayList<>(logResults.size());
    49	
    50	        for (EthLog.LogResult logResult : logResults) {
    51	            if (!(logResult instanceof EthLog.LogObject)) {
    52	                throw new FilterException(
    53	                        "Unexpected result type: " + logResult.get() + " required LogObject");
    54	            }
    55	
    56	            logs.add(((EthLog.LogObject) logResult).get());
    57	        }
    58	
    59	        callback.onEvent(logs);
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    @Override
    63	    protected Optional<Request<?, EthLog>> getFilterLogs(BigInteger filterId) {
    64	        return Optional.of(web3j.ethGetFilterLogs(filterId));
    65	    }
    66	}

    60	    <T> void runTest(EthLog ethLog, Flowable<T> flowable) throws Exception {
    61	        EthFilter ethFilter =
    62	                objectMapper.readValue(
    63	                        "{\n"
    64	                                + "  \"id\":1,\n"
    65	                                + "  \"jsonrpc\": \"2.0\",\n"
    66	                                + "  \"result\": \"0x1\"\n"
    67	                                + "}",
    68	                        EthFilter.class);
    69	
    70	        EthUninstallFilter ethUninstallFilter =
    71	                objectMapper.readValue(
    72	                        "{\"jsonrpc\":\"2.0\",\"id\":1,\"result\":true}", EthUninstallFilter.class);
    73	
    74	        EthLog notFoundFilter =
    75	                objectMapper.readValue(
    76	                        "{\"jsonrpc\":\"2.0\",\"id\":1,"
    77	                                + "\"error\":{\"code\":-32000,\"message\":\"filter not found\"}}",
    78	                        EthLog.class);
    79	
    80	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    81	        List<T> expected = createExpected(ethLog);
    82	        Set<T> results = Collections.synchronizedSet(new HashSet<T>());
    83	
    84	        CountDownLatch transactionLatch = new CountDownLatch(expected.size());
    85	
    86	        CountDownLatch completedLatch = new CountDownLatch(1);
    87	
    88	        when(web3jService.send(any(Request.class), eq(EthFilter.class))).thenReturn(ethFilter);
    89	        when(web3jService.send(any(Request.class), eq(EthLog.class)))
    90	                .thenReturn(ethLog)
    91	                .thenReturn(notFoundFilter)
    92	                .thenReturn(ethLog);
    93	        when(web3jService.send(any(Request.class), eq(EthUninstallFilter.class)))
    94	                .thenReturn(ethUninstallFilter);
    95	
    96	        Disposable subscription =
    97	                flowable.subscribe(
    98	                        result -> {
    99	                            results.add(result);
   100	                            transactionLatch.countDown();
   101	                        },
   102	                        throwable -> fail(throwable.getMessage()),
   103	                        () -> completedLatch.countDown());
   104	
   105	        transactionLatch.await(1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
   106	        assertEquals(results, (new HashSet<>(expected)));
   107	
   108	        subscription.dispose();
   109	
   110	        completedLatch.await(1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
   111	        assertTrue(subscription.isDisposed());
   112	    }
   113

   119

    13	package org.web3j.protocol.scenarios;
    14	
    15	import java.math.BigInteger;
    16	import java.util.Arrays;
    17	import java.util.List;
    18	
    19	import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeAll;
    20	import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
    21	
    22	import org.web3j.EVMTest;
    23	import org.web3j.NodeType;
    24	import org.web3j.abi.EventEncoder;
    25	import org.web3j.abi.FunctionReturnDecoder;
    26	import org.web3j.abi.TypeReference;
    27	import org.web3j.abi.datatypes.Event;
    28	import org.web3j.abi.datatypes.Type;
    29	import org.web3j.abi.datatypes.generated.Uint256;
    30	import org.web3j.protocol.Web3j;
    31	import org.web3j.protocol.core.DefaultBlockParameterName;
    32	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.request.EthFilter;
    33	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.EthLog;
    34	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.Log;
    35	import org.web3j.protocol.core.methods.response.TransactionReceipt;
    36	import org.web3j.test.contract.Fibonacci;
    37	import org.web3j.tx.gas.ContractGasProvider;
    38	
    39	import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertEquals;
    40	import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.assertFalse;
    41	
    42	/** Filter scenario integration tests. */
    43	@EVMTest(type = NodeType.BESU)
    44	public class EventFilterIT extends Scenario {
    45	
    46	    private static Fibonacci fib;
    47	
    48	    @BeforeAll
    49	    public static void setUP(Web3j web3j, ContractGasProvider gasProvider) throws Exception {
    50	
    51	        EventFilterIT.fib = Fibonacci.deploy(web3j, ALICE, gasProvider).send();
    52	        Scenario.web3j = web3j;
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    @Test
    56	    public void testEventFilter() throws Exception {
    57	        TransactionReceipt transactionReceipt = fib.fibonacciNotify(BigInteger.ONE).send();
    58	        List<Log> logs = transactionReceipt.getLogs();
    59	        assertFalse(logs.isEmpty());
    60	        Log log = logs.get(0);
    61	        List<String> topics = log.getTopics();
    62	        assertEquals(topics.size(), (1));
    63	        Event event =
    64	                new Event(
    65	                        "Notify",
    66	                        Arrays.asList(
    67	                                new TypeReference<Uint256>() {}, new TypeReference<Uint256>() {}));
    68	
    69	        // check function signature - we only have a single topic our event signature,
    70	        // there are no indexed parameters in this example
    71	        String encodedEventSignature = EventEncoder.encode(event);
    72	        assertEquals(topics.get(0), (encodedEventSignature));
    73	
    74	        // verify our two event parameters
    75	        List<Type> results =
    76	                FunctionReturnDecoder.decode(log.getData(), event.getNonIndexedParameters());
    77	        results.forEach(it -> assertEquals(it.getValue(), BigInteger.valueOf(1)));
    78	        assertEquals(
    79	                results,
    80	                (Arrays.asList(
    81	                        new Uint256(BigInteger.valueOf(1)), new Uint256(BigInteger.valueOf(1)))));
    82	
    83	        // finally check it shows up in the event filter
    84	        List<EthLog.LogResult> filterLogs = createFilterForEvent(encodedEventSignature);
    85	        assertFalse(filterLogs.isEmpty());
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    private List<EthLog.LogResult> createFilterForEvent(String encodedEventSignature)
    89	            throws Exception {
    90	        EthFilter ethFilter =
    91	                new EthFilter(
    92	                        DefaultBlockParameterName.EARLIEST,
    93	                        DefaultBlockParameterName.LATEST,
    94	                        EventFilterIT.fib.getContractAddress());
    95	
    96	        ethFilter.addSingleTopic(encodedEventSignature);
    97	        EthLog ethLog = web3j.ethGetLogs(ethFilter).send();
    98	        return ethLog.getLogs();
    99	    }
   100	}
